</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="выступает в роли прилагательного">адъектив.</span>, <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;"><a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> полн. <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a></span>, <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="лингвистический термин">лингв.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́й</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:падать.html>па́дает</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ударение.html>ударе́ние</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ударять.html>ударя́емый</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:ударенный.html>Уда́ренный</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:гласный.html>гла́сный</a>. </span></li>
</ul></li>

</ol>
<h4><span id=".D0.A1.D0.B8.D0.BD.D0.BE.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.BC.D1.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Синонимы"><a href = vnd.unilang:синоним.html>Сино́нимы</a></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ударить.html>уда́рить</a> (1036)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ударъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udarŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from Proto-Slavic root <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dōr-</i>. See also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драть.html>драть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dratʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздор.html>раздо́р</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razdór</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ударить.html>уда́рить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udáritʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ударять.html>ударя́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to strike, to knock, to hit, to punch</li>
<li>to butt, to bump</li>
<li>to kick</li>
<li>to set about, to start, to set in</li>
<li>to attack</li></ol>

***удариться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:удариться.html>уда́риться</a> (5309)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ударить.html>уда́рить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udáritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удариться.html>уда́риться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udáritʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ударяться.html>ударя́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hit, to strike <i>(against)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:удариться.html>уда́риться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голово́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>дверь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udáritʹsja</b> golovój o dverʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to strike one's head against the door</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лодка.html>ло́дка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:удариться.html>уда́рилась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скала.html>скалу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lódka <b>udárilasʹ</b> o skalú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the boat struck (against) a rock</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take <i>(to)</i>, to plunge <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:удариться.html>уда́риться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежа́ть</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бегство.html>бе́гство</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udáritʹsja</b> bežátʹ (v bégstvo)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">break into a run</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ударить.html>уда́рить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udáritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удар.html>уда́р</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udár</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ударник.html>уда́рник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udárnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ударник.html>уда́рника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ударник.html>уда́рники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ударник.html>уда́рников</a></b>)

***ударный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ударный.html>уда́рный</a> (8147)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удар.html>уда́р</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udár</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ударный.html>уда́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udárnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)уда́рнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)уда́рней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hit, strike, percussion, shock, impact; percussive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ударный.html>уда́рное</a></b> буре́ние</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udárnoje</b> burénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">percussion drilling</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ударный.html>уда́рный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:инструмент.html>инструме́нт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udárnyj</b> instrumént</i> ― <span class="e-translation">percussion instrument</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ударный.html>уда́рная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:волна.html>волна́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udárnaja</b> volná</i> ― <span class="e-translation">shock wave</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ударный.html>уда́рный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кратер.html>кра́тер</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udárnyj</b> kráter/krátɛr</i> ― <span class="e-translation">impact crater</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>accelerated, shock <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of work</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ударный.html>уда́рная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бригада.html>брига́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udárnaja</b> brigáda</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>shock</b> brigade</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ударный.html>уда́рные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:темп.html>те́мпы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udárnyje</b> tɛ́mpy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">accelerated tempo, high tempo</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shock
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ударный.html>уда́рные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>ча́сти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udárnyje</b> části</i> ― <span class="e-translation">shock troops</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">linguistics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> stressed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ударный.html>уда́рный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слог.html>слог</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udárnyj</b> slog</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>stressed</b> syllable</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>effective, giving a quick result
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ударный.html>уда́рная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:доза.html>до́за</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udárnaja</b> dóza</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>effective</b> dose <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of medicine</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>particularly important, necessary <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of business, work, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ударный.html>уда́рное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:задание.html>зада́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udárnoje</b> zadánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>necessary</b> task</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ударить.html>уда́рить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udáritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***ударяться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ударяться.html>ударя́ться</a> (15850)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ударять.html>ударя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udarjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ударяться.html>ударя́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udarjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удариться.html>уда́риться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hit, to strike <i>(against)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take <i>(to)</i>, to plunge <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ударяться.html>ударя́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крайность.html>кра́йность</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udarjátʹsja</b> v krájnostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run to an extreme</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ударяться.html>ударя́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одно́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крайность.html>кра́йности</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>другу́ю</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udarjátʹsja</b> iz odnój krájnosti v drugúju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rush/go from one extreme to another</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ударять.html>ударя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udarjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***ударяющий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ударять.html>ударя́ющий</a> (8998)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ударять.html>ударя́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udarjájuščij</span>)
</p>

***удаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:удаться.html>уда́ться</a> (552)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">datʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удаться.html>уда́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удаваться.html>удава́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn out well, to be a success
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сразу.html>сра́зу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:видно.html>ви́дно</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:праздник.html>пра́здник</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:удаться.html>удался́</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Srázu býlo vídno: prázdnik <b>udalsjá</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It was immediately evident: the festival <b>was a success</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to succeed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:удаться.html>удало́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:решить.html>реши́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́ту</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задача.html>зада́чу</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mne <b>udalósʹ</b> rešítʹ étu zadáču.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I <b>managed</b> to solve this problem/task.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выйти.html>вы́йти</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výjti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получиться.html>получи́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">polučítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:довестись.html>довести́сь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dovestísʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удача.html>уда́ча</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">udáča</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***удвоить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:удвоить.html>удво́ить</a> (23839)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двое.html>дво́е</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dvóje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удвоить.html>удво́ить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udvóitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">удва́ивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to double, to redouble
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:удвоить.html>удво́ить</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:усилие.html>уси́лия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udvóitʹ</b> (svoí) usílija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to redouble one's efforts</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">linguistics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to reduplicate</li></ol>

***удел.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:удел.html>уде́л</a> (14256)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удел.html>уде́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udél</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удел.html>уде́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удел.html>уде́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удел.html>уде́лов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удельный.html>уде́льный</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lot, destiny</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> appanage, independent principality <i>(in mediaeval Russia)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***уделить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уделить.html>удели́ть</a> (12671)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делить.html>дели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">delítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уделить.html>удели́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udelítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уделять.html>уделя́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to allot, to allocate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:уделить.html>удели́те</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тридцать.html>три́дцать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:секунда.html>секу́нд</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:пожалуйста.html>пожа́луйста</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Udelíte</b> mne trídcatʹ sekúnd, požálujsta.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Spare me thirty seconds, please.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:удельный.html>уде́льный</a> (12585)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удел.html>уде́л</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udél</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удельный.html>уде́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udélʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> specific
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:удельный.html>уде́льная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:теплота.html>теплота́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udélʹnaja</b> teplotá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">specific heat</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>per capita, per unit
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:удельный.html>уде́льное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:потребление.html>потребле́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udélʹnoje</b> potreblénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">consumption per capita</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удельный.html>уде́льный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вес.html>ве́с</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">udélʹnyj vés</i> ― <span class="e-translation">percentage, proportion</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> appanage <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">related to an <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удел.html>уде́л</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udél</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***уделявшийся.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уделяться.html>уделя́вшийся</a> (23317)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уделяться.html>уделя́вшийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udeljávšijsja</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уделяться.html>уделя́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udeljátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уделять.html>уделя́ть</a> (11822)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уделить.html>удели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udelítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уделять.html>уделя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udeljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уделить.html>удели́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to allot, to allocate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:уделять.html>уделя́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спорт.html>спо́рту</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná <b>udeljájet</b> vrémja spórtu.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">She finds time for sports.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">She <b>allocates</b> time for sports.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:уделять.html>уделя́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:внимание.html>внима́ние</a> кому́-либо/чему́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>udeljátʹ</b> vnimánije komú-libo/čemú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pay attention to someone/something</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***уделяющий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уделять.html>уделя́ющий</a> (11822)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***удержать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:удержать.html>удержа́ть</a> (4185)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">deržátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удержать.html>удержа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uderžátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удерживать.html>уде́рживать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to retain, to hold</li>
<li>to hold back, to keep (from), to withhold</li>
<li>to suppress</li>
<li>to deduct, to keep back</li></ol>

***удержаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:удержаться.html>удержа́ться</a> (3181)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удержать.html>удержа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uderžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удержаться.html>удержа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uderžátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удерживаться.html>уде́рживаться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to keep, to remain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:удержаться.html>удержа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>нога́х</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uderžátʹsja</b> na nogáx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to keep one's feet; remain on one's feet</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:удержаться.html>удержа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:седло.html>седле́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uderžátʹsja</b> v sedlé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to keep/stay in the saddle</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to hold one's ground, to hold out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неприятель.html>неприя́тель</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стараться.html>стара́лся</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:удержаться.html>удержа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:река.html>реке́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">neprijátelʹ starálsja <b>uderžátʹsja</b> na reké</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the enemy tried to hold out [make a stand] on the river</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to keep <i>(from)</i>, to refrain <i>(from)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:удержаться.html>удержа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:соблазн.html>собла́зна</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uderžátʹsja</b> ot soblázna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to resist the temptation</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удерживаться.html>уде́рживаться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:курение.html>куре́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">udérživatʹsja ot kurénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">refrain from smoking</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:удержаться.html>удержа́ться</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nelʹzjá <b>uderžátʹsja</b> (ot)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">one cannot help</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́г</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:удержаться.html>удержа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смех.html>сме́ха</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on ne mog <b>uderžátʹsja</b> ot sméxa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he couldn't help [refrain from] laughing</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удержать.html>удержа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uderžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***удерживать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:удерживать.html>уде́рживать</a> (4414)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удержать.html>удержа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uderžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удерживать.html>уде́рживать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udérživatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удержать.html>удержа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to retain, to hold</li>
<li>to hold back, to keep (from), to withhold</li>
<li>to suppress</li>
<li>to deduct, to keep back</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удерживать.html>уде́рживать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udérživatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удерживаться.html>уде́рживаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">udérživatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удержаться.html>удержа́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to keep, to remain</li>
<li>to hold one's ground, to hold out</li>
<li>to keep <i>(from)</i>, to refrain <i>(from)</i>

<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удерживать.html>уде́рживать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udérživatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
